            AFTERNOON AT THE RACE TRACK - Description of the internal state of the problem

 Stat St0      Am0 St1 Am1  St2 Am2  St3 Am3  RN  St0 Len0  St1 Len1  St2 Len2  St3 Len3               
                                         Race RN Status

 #  #### ### ### ### ### ### ### ### ### ### ## ### ### ### ## ### ### ### ## ### ### ### ## ### ###

Legend:
Stat - manager/broker state
St# - spectator/better state (# - 0 .. 3)
Am# - spectator/better amount of money she has presently (# - 0 .. 3)
RN - race number
St# - horse/jockey pair state in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
Len# - horse/jockey pair maximum moving length per iteration step in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
RN - race number
Dist - race track distance in present race
BS# - spectator/better bet selection in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
BA# - spectator/better bet amount in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
Od# - horse/jockey pair winning probability in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
N# - horse/jockey pair iteration step number in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
Ps# - horse/jockey pair track position in present race (# - 0 .. 3)
SD# - horse/jockey pair standing at the end of present race (# - 0 .. 3)
STEv - START_THE_EVENT state (broker)
OTEv - OPENING_THE_EVENT state (broker)
AnNR - ANNOUNCING_NEXT_RACE state (broker)
WaFB - WAITING_FOR_BETS state (broker)
WaFH - WAITING_FOR_HORSES state (broker)
SuTR - SUPERVISING_THE_RACE state (broker)
RRes - REPORTING_RESULTS state (broker)
SACc - SETTLING_ACCOUNTS state (broker)
PHAB - START_THE_EVENT state (broker)
STEv - PLAYING_HOST_AT_THE_BAR state (broker)
WRS - WAITING_FOR_A_RACE_TO_START state (spectator)
ATH - APPRAISING_THE_HORSES state (spectator)
PAB - PLACING_A_BET state (spectator)
WAR - WATCHING_A_RACE state (spectator)
CRE - CHECKING_RESULTS state (spectator)
CTG - COLLECTING_THE_GAINS state (spectator)
CEL - CELEBRATING state (spectator)
ATS - AT_THE_STABLE state (horse)
ATP - AT_THE_PADDOCK state (horse)
ASL - AT_THE_START_LINE state (horse)
RUN - RUNNING state (horse)
AFL - AT_THE_FINISH_LINE state (horse)
NDS - NOT_DEFINED_STATE (broker/spectator/horse)
